[Location] It is right by the West Lake, next to the provincial government, more than 10 minutes walk from the Broken Bridge, more than 10 minutes walk from Wulin Gate and Fengqi Road subway station, and the bus stop is right outside. There will be traffic jams near the West Lake during holidays. We took the bus and subway to and from the scenic spots in Hangzhou for a few days, which is faster and more convenient than taking a taxi. At night, we can also take a leisurely walk around the West Lake, which feels great! 
[Facilities] The decoration is very decent, the facilities are very new, and it feels very clean and bright. The curtains are automatic and the toilet is smart. 
[Service] This is to be blown up. You can believe that the waiter will leave a note by hand after cleaning every day, and it is not a mechanical greeting, but really helping customers with heart. For example, when our dirty clothes were piled together, they reminded us that there was a self-service laundry room on the negative first floor, and they also put a mat on the ground for our suitcases. The service is simply responsive. When I asked the front desk about the lack of chopsticks when ordering takeout, the young lady could have directly replied that there were no chopsticks, but she actually ran back to the lounge to give me a portion of the tableware she usually left. We ordered too many dishes the night before and packed them back to the hotel. The next morning, the restaurant boy didn't mind the trouble to help us heat them up in the kitchen. I was a little touched!
[Summary] It feels like a government guesthouse that is also used by civilians in its spare time. Behind it is the Great Hall of the People of Zhejiang Province, and there are special police standing guard. The sense of security is overwhelming. Many people in the lobby wear party badges and their attitudes are very friendly. There is an inexplicable sense of intimacy. The service is friendly and in place, the transportation location is convenient, the facilities are clean and hygienic, and it is recommended with five stars!
[Sharing] We spent a total of three days, one day around West Lake, one day hiking from Jiuxi to Lingyin Temple, and half a day in Xixi Wetland Park. The itinerary is just right and the experience is awesome. For your reference

Bai Duo felt unhappy at the time and immediately canceled the order. But because the time was short, it would take time to select the hotel again, so I booked this hotel again (brothers, it turns out that hotels without the concept of integrity cannot be selected). When I checked in at the front desk of the hotel, I asked which floor the breakfast was on. Then the front desk told me that the hotel did not have a buffet due to the lack of people staying in the hotel. I needed to order breakfast with the front desk and have it delivered to the room. I was very unhappy (brothers who often travel on business know this) , the reason why we choose a five-star hotel for vacation is naturally to enjoy the service and enjoy the free buffet), but the so-called Great Hall of the People Hotel easily told me that it could not open a buffet because of the low occupancy rate. Then the next room (No window) I casually asked if it was possible to upgrade, and the front desk gave me an official answer: "It seems impossible to upgrade!" OK, I endure it. Then he collected the pre-sale deposit and told me that the room fee was 533 and he would charge me a 500 consumption deposit. I can understand this. It is normal to receive a consumption deposit when booking a hotel on Ctrip. But the problem is that I just paid the 500 deposit, and then they told me to charge a deposit for the room fee. I was really angry! ***You don‚Äôt take your customers seriously! He repeatedly gave in and entertained us! Playing with consumers in this way, and then having a blunt service attitude, even a township guest house wouldn't be like this! What I regret most is that I should have canceled the order and not been angry if I didn't check in. But considering that I was traveling with my family, I decided to stay. It was normal for the waiter at the back to wait for me when I came back in the evening (his work was not finished yet) and ask me what I would do for breakfast. When I returned from a run in the morning, the lobby manager also came over to ask me about the breakfast delivery. Objectively speaking, I didn't want to embarrass the individual. I told them that their hotel's behavior (fraudulent behavior) came first, and the front desk's blunt attitude and lack of friendliness was an incentive that made people unable to accept it anymore.
I rarely say so much, but this time I was really unhappy. The hotel's arrogance ruined my Mid-Autumn Festival and my usual good mood in Hangzhou! So here I would like to remind colleagues who pay attention to service experience, and also remind the person in charge of the Ctrip platform to take the initiative to contact me after seeing this. Is the platform aware of this kind of consumer fraud in advance? Are you responsible for informing customers in advance? Of course, this is more to remind colleagues who pay attention to travel experience when going out: similar to hotels (guest houses), you must be cautious, and it is more reliable to stay in brand hotels.
By the way, after I checked into the hotel, a man called me and told me to change to a room with a window. A person who looked like a lobby manager at the hotel also communicated with me and admitted the problems with his hotel, and prepared some preparations before leaving. I received two so-called gifts, but I refused!
Because I really didn‚Äôt feel the sincerity, and I didn‚Äôt feel the feeling of being at home like at the Scholars Hotel, so what I thought in my mind was: Even if you give me money in the future, I will never stay in a hotel like this!
I understand everything.
